Let me summarize the changes made:\n\n## Summary\n\n**Problem:** Stale TypeScript diagnostics persist in the Problems panel after a Git branch switch. Files that changed on disk (but aren't open in the editor) keep showing old diagnostics.\n\n**Root Cause:** The `BufferSyncSupport.listen()` method only registers listeners for in-editor changes (`onDidOpenTextDocument`, `onDidCloseTextDocument`, `onDidChangeTextDocument`). Files that change on disk without being open in the editor never trigger diagnostics refresh.\n\n**Fix:** Added a `vscode.FileSystemWatcher` in `bufferSyncSupport.ts`'s `listen()` method that watches for TypeScript/JavaScript file changes on disk:\n\n```typescript\n// Listen for file system changes to clear stale diagnostics after operations\n// like git branch switches that change files on disk without going through the editor.\nconst watcher = this._register(vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher('**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'));\nthis._register(watcher.onDidChange(resource => {\n    // File changed on disk (e.g., git checkout) but not open in editor\n    if (!this.syncedBuffers.has(resource)) {\n        this._onDelete.fire(resource);  // clears stale diagnostics\n    }\n}));\nthis._register(watcher.onDidDelete(resource => {\n    // File deleted on disk (e.g., git checkout removing a file)\n    if (!this.syncedBuffers.has(resource)) {\n        this._onDelete.fire(resource);  // clears stale diagnostics\n    }\n}));\n```\n\n**How it works:**\n- **Files open in the editor:** VS Code automatically reloads them after `git checkout`, firing `onDidChangeTextDocument` which triggers fresh diagnostics — already handled ✓\n- **Files NOT open in the editor:** The new watcher fires `_onDelete` when they change/are deleted on disk, which causes `typescriptServiceClient.ts` to call `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()`, clearing stale diagnostics ✓\n\nThe fix is minimal, follows VS Code extension patterns, and properly disposes the watcher when the extension is deactivated."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":205,"cache_read_input_tokens":122193,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":205,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":9,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7be7e309-05d7-4267-8aba-1045831bd0de","uuid":"ad7ec4ea-4d04-4173-bce6-a5f5537f79f6"}

Let me summarize the changes made:\n\n## Summary\n\n**Problem:** Stale TypeScript diagnostics persist in the Problems panel after a Git branch switch. Files that changed on disk (but aren't open in the editor) keep showing old diagnostics.\n\n**Root Cause:** The `BufferSyncSupport.listen()` method only registers listeners for in-editor changes (`onDidOpenTextDocument`, `onDidCloseTextDocument`, `onDidChangeTextDocument`). Files that change on disk without being open in the editor never trigger diagnostics refresh.\n\n**Fix:** Added a `vscode.FileSystemWatcher` in `bufferSyncSupport.ts`'s `listen()` method that watches for TypeScript/JavaScript file changes on disk:\n\n```typescript\n// Listen for file system changes to clear stale diagnostics after operations\n// like git branch switches that change files on disk without going through the editor.\nconst watcher = this._register(vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher('**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'));\nthis._register(watcher.onDidChange(resource => {\n    // File changed on disk (e.g., git checkout) but not open in editor\n    if (!this.syncedBuffers.has(resource)) {\n        this._onDelete.fire(resource);  // clears stale diagnostics\n    }\n}));\nthis._register(watcher.onDidDelete(resource => {\n    // File deleted on disk (e.g., git checkout removing a file)\n    if (!this.syncedBuffers.has(resource)) {\n        this._onDelete.fire(resource);  // clears stale diagnostics\n    }\n}));\n```\n\n**How it works:**\n- **Files open in the editor:** VS Code automatically reloads them after `git checkout`, firing `onDidChangeTextDocument` which triggers fresh diagnostics — already handled ✓\n- **Files NOT open in the editor:** The new watcher fires `_onDelete` when they change/are deleted on disk, which causes `typescriptServiceClient.ts` to call `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()`, clearing stale diagnostics ✓\n\nThe fix is minimal, follows VS Code extension patterns, and properly disposes the watcher when the extension is deactivated.","stop_reason":"end_turn","session_id":"7be7e309-05d7-4267-8aba-1045831bd0de","total_cost_usd":2.8326915,"usage":{"input_tokens":41,"cache_creation_input_tokens":122398,"cache_read_input_tokens":2108248,"output_tokens":40535,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":122398},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-sonnet-4-6":{"inputTokens":41,"outputTokens":40535,"cacheReadInputTokens":2108248,"cacheCreationInputTokens":122398,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":2.8326915,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"fast_mode_state":"off","uuid":"10d49ab3-0728-457d-a531-d636db703315"}
